<user_name>Connor Byram</user_name><Response>None<//Response>< review>
I was in San Diego on vacation. I had a liquid spill on my Macbook. They took it in immediately and did a chemical clean. They got my Macbook up and running in 2 days. They were very friendly, however their communication could be better. I was initially told the repair would be same-day. I had to reach out multiple times to get updates on my computer and to receive a report on the findings/diagnosis after I picked up my computer. I also did not like that they put 3 stickers on my Mac, though they came off easily. Overall, I had a good experience and would return. Improvement could be made by being more upfront/realistic about repair times. They would also do better to provide the customer with an in-depth review of what will be done when the drop off is made, and provide diagnosis/repair paperwork to the customer upon pickup.<//review>

<review>I'm very disappointed with this business. I've stored my stuff here for about 3 or 4 years. Everything was great in the beginning, great rate, great customer service and very helpful. I started out paying $49 a month for a 5' x 10' (small unit) and occasionally I would be late on a payment because of the due date and my pay day schedule, so naturally I knew I would have to pay a $10 late fee. I never complained. A man that works there called me to tell me about my payment and I just didn't have the extra $10 at the time. He was very sweet and told me if I go online and just pay the regular amount, minus the $10 he would then go in and waive the late fee! I was so grateful. He proceeded to tell me they're really only allowed to do that twice a year but they really shouldn't. I totally understood. Well after one year of storing my stuff there, the monthly rate went up by $10... Another year went by and it went up by another $10!!! I'm now paying $71 a month and remember it's a 5'x10'!!! So this month I was going to log in to my account and couldn't access it. I tried resetting my password I even sent in a "contact us" request with a message about what was going on and surprise surprise I never got a call or email from them... I had to keep trying and eventually figured it out (days later). Once I logged in I noticed they were charging me a $15 late fee. I'm absolutely floored, Dave just called me to ask about my payment and I mentioned the late fee amount, I asked him if he could waive the $15 late fee like he mentioned before, since I've only done that one time in 3-4 years, he said no he cannot. So it looks like I'll be making my final payment of $86 dollars for a very small unit and taking my belongings elsewhere. So upset with this business right now. I wouldn't be surprised to see it shut down very soon with the way they treat a long time customer. Goodbye public storage :)</review>< Response>

<Text>While I think the general view is that this is a typical storage place...I have rented at a few and this is the first that doesn't allow you to use the recycle and garbage bins which is insane. I understand a case by case basis and they unlock for you or don't depending on what you have, but some flattened boxes? Insane. I was told its company policy...yet another public storage has allowed it.Do apartment complexes tell their tenants they cant use the dumpsters? No, because that would be ridiculous. I called to ask for a suggestion of where to dump extra boxes as I'm not familiar with this area, and again...it makes no sense why I can't dump at the property...and while not the girls fault for not knowing because she too is new to the area...i feel it was her responsibility as an individual expected to provide customer service to find out. At the very least, try. Ask another property, ask your manager, ask another storage renter, do something. So as far as I'm   concerned, and having a relationship with public storage since 1998-1999, I will no longer be renting with them. < Text>
This location is experiencing growing pains at least I hope.

Food quality was on par to other CFAs so the star rating is relative to better experiences.

Arrived at the start of lunch time rush, line inside was only halfway to the door but still only had two cashiers working. 10 mins to put in order and 16 mins to receive food, seems like the norm as there were plenty of people sitting and waiting for their food. By the time I left, line was to the door and drive thru line had overflowed onto the street, which along with blocking traffic also blocks those that just want to park in the parking lot.

I plan to reassess in the future to see if improvements have been made.

4/14/20 Update: while their setup for curbside pick up, I beat the lunch time rush and my order came out incorrect. Ordered and paid for spicy chicken sandwich but received an original chicken sandwich<//Text>
